	}
	title = CHI.earlygame.000.t
	desc = CHI.earlygame.000.d

		complete_national_focus = CHI_last_bastion_of_chinese_socialism
	}
}

country_event = { #The Harvest of 1936
	id = CHI.earlygame.001
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event CHI.earlygame.001" }
	title = CHI.earlygame.001.t
	desc = CHI.earlygame.001.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_economic

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by CHI.earlygame.000, should be on June 24th, 1936

	option = { #They'll have to get used to these changes for the greater good.
		name = CHI.earlygame.001.a
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_command_power = 30
		add_stability = -0.10
	}

	option = { #Divert new recruits to get some moral training in the fields.
		name = CHI.earlygame.001.b
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_manpower = -100000 #You have around 130k after you secure your cores during League War
		army_experience = -30
		add_war_support = 0.05
	}
}

country_event = { #The Secretive Retainer
	id = CHI.earlygame.002
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event CHI.earlygame.002" }
	title = CHI.earlygame.002.t
	desc = CHI.earlygame.002.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_intelligence

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by event lepcollapse.19
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Is that so?
		name = CHI.earlygame.002.a
		add_intel = {
			target = CHI
			civilian_intel = 10
			army_intel = 15
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				name = CHI_totalist_juntong_generic
				long_name = CHI_totalist_juntong_generic_long
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Dai Chunfeng"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHI_DAI_CHUNFENG_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_CHI_Dai_Chunfeng.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = socialist_security_state_subtype
			}
			CHI = {
				country_event = { id = CHI.earlygame.003 days = 3 } #Spies and Secrets in the League War
			}
		}
	}
}

###- Early Game Events Triggered By On-Actions (200-299) -###

country_event = { # Return of the Central Committee - fired by completing capture of Xiamen
	id = CHI.earlygame.200
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event CHI.earlygame.200" }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			XXA = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_id = 2295
							has_id = 2280
							has_id = 2299
							has_id = 2279
						}
					}
					set_nationality = INT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	title = CHI.earlygame.200.t
	desc = CHI.earlygame.200.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_wang_jingwei_plane_takeoff

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = CHI.earlygame.200.a
		division_template = {
			name = "Dúli Bubing Lü"    # Represents: small professional units for early 2nd NRA
			division_names_group = CHI_INF_04
			regiments = {
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 } # Note: Chinese divisions were brigade-sized compared to other nations' armies
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 } # Lit. 'Independent Infantry Brigade' in Mandarin (tone inconsistencies match HOI4 Vanilla)
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
			}
		}
		division_template = {
			name = "Committee's Own"
			division_names_group = CHI_INF_02
			regiments = {
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				artillery_brigade = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				artillery_brigade = { x = 2 y = 2 }
			}
		}
		802 = {
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"Committee's Own\" division_template = \"Committee's Own\" start_experience_factor = 1.0"
				prioritize_location = 802
				owner = CHI
			}
		}
		remove_country_leader_trait = CHI_exiled_chairman
		INT = {
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 2279 }
				CHI_recruit_general_effect = yes 
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 2295 }
				CHI_recruit_general_effect = yes 
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 2280 }
				CHI_recruit_general_effect = yes 
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 2299 }
				CHI_recruit_general_effect = yes 
			}
		}
		LEP = {
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 2278 }
				CHI_recruit_general_effect = yes 
			}

		add_ideas = CHI_mac_idea

		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		add_state_core = 613
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_we_will_lose_league_war_factories_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_focus_tree_will_change_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_offsite_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = CHI_foreign_offmap_mils_var
			}
			add_offsite_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = CHI_foreign_offmap_civs_var
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_socialist_government = yes
					OR = {
						tag = FRA
						tag = ENG
						tag = NOR
						tag = BHC
						tag = SRI
						AND = {
							is_major = yes
							is_in_faction_with = FRA
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = CHI.midgame.600 days = 3 } #Report from the MMIC
			}
		}
	}
}

	option = { #Empower Zhou Enlai's Teke

				factor = 1000

			}
		}
		CHI_RCA_medium_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CHI_chose_teke_flag
			country_event = { id = CHI.midgame.209 days = 1 random_days = 1 } #Heroics of Teke
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = CHI_Zhou_Enlai_eco_rso
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "La Resistance" } }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_ideas = CHI_teke_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_intelligence_agency = no }
			create_intelligence_agency = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_form_department } }
			upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_form_department
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_psycho_warfare } }
			upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_psycho_warfare
		}
		else = { add_political_power = 50 }
	}
	option = { #Empower Dai's BIS

				factor = 1000

		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "La Resistance" }
			show_ideas_tooltip = CHI_Dai_Chunfeng_sec_tot_lar
			else = {
				show_ideas_tooltip = CHI_Dai_Chunfeng_sec_tot
			}
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "La Resistance" } }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_ideas = CHI_bis_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_intelligence_agency = no }
			create_intelligence_agency = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_army_department } }
			upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_army_department
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_invisible_ink } }

		}
		else = { add_political_power = 50 }

				factor = 3
				strength_ratio = {

					ratio < 0.5
				}

			}

			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}

				factor = 3
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 2
				}

	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_successful_northern_expedition_flag
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by decision CHI_NAP_with_rkmt_decision
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_war_with = CHI }
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = CHI.midgame.911.a #The corrupt Beiyang warlords must fall! We accept.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.75
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 3
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = { #RKMT don't want multiple wars
				factor = 3
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = { #If the political situation in China has drastically changed
				factor = 5
				OR = {
					QIE = { exists = no }
					FNG = { exists = no }
					any_other_country = {
						is_chinese_tag = yes
						has_war_with = JAP
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				CHI = { has_idea = CHI_Sun_Fo_hog_sli }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = CHI_ally_betrayal option = CHI_ALLY_BETRAYAL_NEVER }
			}
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { CHI = { has_idea = CHI_Sun_Fo_hog_sli } }
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -40
		}
		set_country_flag = CHI_RKT_NAP_flag
		FROM = { hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.midgame.912 days = 3 } } } #[FROM.GetNameDefCap] Accepts Our Pact!
	}
	option = {
		name = CHI.midgame.911.b #Wang is nothing but an Internationale bootlicker!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1.3
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 3
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 2
				}
			}
			modifier = { #RKMT less likely to agree if KMT is choking them
				factor = 3
				all_neighbor_country = {
					OR = {
						tag = FROM
						is_subject_of = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Measure # of RKMT Puppets
				factor = 5
				num_subjects > 4
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_hates_govt
		}
		FROM = { hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.midgame.913 days = 3 } } } #[FROM.GetNameDefCap] Rejects Our Pact!
	}
}

					is_chinese_tag = yes
					china_is_potential_government = no
				}
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = CHI
					modifier = KR_pleased
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #The Party has room to grow a little bit.
		name = CHI.lategame.061.b

		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.02 }
		if = {
			limit = { CHI_is_phase_four_trigger = no }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		CHI_CRS_medium_effect = yes
	}

	option = { #We have no use for them during tutelage.
		name = CHI.lategame.061.c
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }

		CHI_RCA_medium_effect = yes

country_event = { #A League Divided
	id = CHI.lategame.207
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event CHI.lategame.207" }
	title = CHI.lategame.207.t
	desc = {
		text = CHI.lategame.207.d.LCS
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = LCS_shattered_flag } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = CHI.lategame.207.d.ORT
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_ORT_dom_flag }
	}
	desc = {
		text = CHI.lategame.207.d.RAD
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_RAD_dom_flag }
	}
	desc = {
		text = CHI.lategame.207.d.WRD
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_WRD_dom_flag }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_worker

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by focus CHI_third_national_congress
	timeout_days = 7

	option = { #We stand against reactionary subversion!
		name = CHI.lategame.207.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_WRD_dom_flag
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_ORT_dom_flag
					has_country_flag = CHI_pac_lcs_alignment_flag
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_lcs_divided_rca_tt
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = LCS_shattered_flag } }
			if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.05 }
				CHI_RCA_mega_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.03 }
				CHI_RCA_large_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.01 }
				CHI_RCA_medium_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				CHI_RCA_small_effect = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = CHI_pac_lcs_alignment_flag
						has_country_flag = CHI_rca_lcs_alignment_flag
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = CHI_rca_lcs_alignment_flag
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_ORT_dom_flag }
			if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.15 }
				CHI_RCA_mega_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.10 }
				CHI_RCA_large_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.05 }
				CHI_RCA_medium_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				CHI_RCA_small_effect = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = CHI_pac_lcs_alignment_flag
						has_country_flag = CHI_rca_lcs_alignment_flag
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = CHI_rca_lcs_alignment_flag
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.30 }
				CHI_RCA_mega_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.20 }
				CHI_RCA_large_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.10 }
				CHI_RCA_medium_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				CHI_RCA_small_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Wang has become too much of a danger!
		name = CHI.lategame.207.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_RAD_dom_flag
				AND = {

				}
			}
		}

		if = {

			}

country_event = { #The Long Shadow
	id = CHI.lategame.209
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event CHI.lategame.209" }
	title = CHI.lategame.209.t
	desc = CHI.lategame.209.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_CRS_meeting

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by focus CHI_third_national_congress
	timeout_days = 7

	option = { #Such Buffoonery!
		name = CHI.lategame.209.a

		set_temp_variable = { CHI_rad_stab_var = CHI_radicalism_var } #Should be between 0-1
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_rad_stab_var = -0.5 } #Should be between -0.5-0
		add_stability = CHI_rad_stab_var

		#Half of radicalism is distributed across radical factions.
		#If CSP Radicals can contest radicalism, only a quarter goes to CRS. Otherwise, half goes to CRS.
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_rad_pop_var = CHI_radicalism_var } #Should be between 0-1
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_RAD_dom_flag }
			multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_rad_pop_var = 0.25 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = CHI_rad_pop_var }
			add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = CHI_rad_pop_var }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_long_shadow_csp_tt
		}
		else = {
			multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_rad_pop_var = 0.50 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = CHI_rad_pop_var }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_long_shadow_tt
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Impeachment Vote
	id = CHI.lategame.210
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event CHI.lategame.210" }
	title = CHI.lategame.210.t
	desc = CHI.lategame.210.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_song_qingling_speech_party_conference_2

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by focus CHI_third_national_congress
	timeout_days = 7

	option = { #The die is cast...
		name = CHI.lategame.210.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_impeachment_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = CHI_PATH option = DEFAULT } #NOT HAVING THE DEFAULT GAMERULE RIGS THE OUTCOME OF THE GAME FOR THE AI
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = CHI_radicalism_var
						value = power_balance_value
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.350 days = 1 } } #Chaos on the Convention Floor
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					CHI_PAC_winning_trigger = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.300 days = 1 } } #Wang is ousted from power!
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					CHI_RCA_winning_trigger = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.250 days = 1 } } #Wang Carries the Day!
			}
			else = {
				#fallback
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.350 days = 1 } } #Chaos on the Convention Floor
			}
		}
		else = {
			#Cheaty, cheaty gamerules
			if = {
				limit = {
					CHI_gamerule_scenario_3 = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.350 days = 1 } } #Chaos on the Convention Floor
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						CHI_gamerule_song_victory = yes
						CHI_gamerule_csp_victory = yes
						CHI_gamerule_deng_victory = yes
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.300 days = 1 } } #Wang is ousted from power!
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					CHI_gamerule_wang_victory = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.250 days = 1 } } #Wang Carries the Day!
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_power_balance = { id = CHI_power_balance }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Wang carries the Day
	id = CHI.lategame.250
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event CHI.lategame.250" }
	title = CHI.lategame.250.t
	desc = CHI.lategame.250.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_wang_jingwei_mad
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes #triggered from CHI.lategame.210, from 3rd National Congress
	timeout_days = 7

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.251 days = 3 } #Assault on Wuhan
			if = {
				limit = { UPC = { is_subject_of = CHI } }
				UPC = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.291 days = 1 } } #A Rebellion Flares in Fujian!
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RKT = { is_subject_of = CHI } }
				RKT = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.293 days = 1 } } #Rebellion Breaks Out in Fujian!
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI.lategame.250.a
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		CHI_setup_chen_gongbo_hog = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_soc_dem_stab_loss_tt
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_party_pop_stab_loss_temp_var = party_popularity@social_democrat }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_party_pop_stab_loss_temp_var = -0.5 }
		add_stability = CHI_party_pop_stab_loss_temp_var
		CHI_purge_PAC_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_PAC_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_RF_generals_effect = yes
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	timeout_days = 7

	option = {
		name = CHI.lategame.300.a
		set_politics = { ruling_party = social_democrat }		
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = CHI_Deng_Yanda_hog_sde
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var = party_popularity@radical_socialist }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var = 0.75 }
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_neg_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var = CHI_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_neg_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var = -1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = CHI_neg_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = CHI_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.301 days = 3 } #The Rising Backlash
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.302 days = 7 } #RCA strikes back
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.303 days = 15 } #The Coalition wavers
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.304 days = 18 } #The Breaking Point
			if = {
				limit = { UPC = { is_subject_of = CHI } }
				UPC = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.341 days = 20 } } #Wang Jingwei Deposed!
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RKT = { is_subject_of = CHI } }
				RKT = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.343 days = 20 } } #Victory of the Opposition!
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = CHI.lategame.354 #The Lesser Sun

	timeout_days = 7

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { UPC = { is_subject_of = CHI } }
				UPC = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.391 days = 3 random_days = 4 } } #The End of the Kuomintang-Federalist Alliance
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RKT = { is_subject_of = CHI } }

				limit = {
					OR = {

						#Only large non-Chinese subjects can influence CHI politics
						strength_ratio = { tag = CHI ratio > 0.5 }
						naval_strength_ratio = { tag = CHI ratio > 1 }
						ic_ratio = { tag = CHI ratio > 0.5 }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.360 days = 10 } #The Kuomintang Civil War
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CHI = { has_character = CHI_MMIC_theorist_idea } }

			}
		}
	}

					CHI_gamerule_deng_victory = yes
				}
			}
		}
		CHI_recruit_RF_generals_effect = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = 0.03 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.03 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = 0.04 }
		CHI_gov_civ_war_add_3_effect = yes
		CHI_pac_civ_war_add_3_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.370 days = 3 } #The Garrison at Wuhan
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.375 days = 15 } #Battles Along the Coastline
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.376 days = 30 } #Unrest in Nanjing
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.390 days = 40 } #The Dust Settles
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = CHI.lategame.354.b #Declare Martial Law
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				check_variable = { CHI_crs_civ_war_var > CHI_gov_civ_war_var }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				CHI_crs_won_civil_war_trigger = yes #In this case "winning" not won

		}

					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = CHI.lategame.376 #Unrest in Nanjing
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event CHI.lategame.376" }
	title = CHI.lategame.376.t
	desc = CHI.lategame.376.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_riot3
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	timeout_days = 7

	option = {
		name = CHI.lategame.376.a #He reaches his bunker safely...
		trigger = { check_variable = { CHI_gov_civ_war_var > CHI_crs_civ_war_var } }
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var = CHI_pac_civ_war_var }
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var
			min = 1 #It will always boost a faction
		}
		add_to_variable = { CHI_gov_civ_war_var = CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var }
		set_variable = { CHI_crs_civ_war_var = 0 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_nanjing_unrest_gov_victory_tt
	}
	option = {
		name = CHI.lategame.376.b #The CRS takes control!
		trigger = { check_variable = { CHI_gov_civ_war_var < CHI_crs_civ_war_var } }
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var = CHI_gov_civ_war_var }
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var
			min = 1 #It will always boost a faction
		}
		add_to_variable = { CHI_crs_civ_war_var = CHI_gov_civ_war_var }
		set_variable = { CHI_gov_civ_war_var = 0 }		
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = { CHI_hu_zongnan_in_power = no }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Hu Zongnan"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHI_HU_ZONGNAN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_CHI_Hu_Zongnan_KR.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = red_junta_subtype
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_nanjing_unrest_crs_takeover_tt
	}
}

		trigger = { check_variable = { CHI_crs_civ_war_var < CHI_rca_civ_war_var } }
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var = CHI_gov_civ_war_var }
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var
			min = 1 #It will always boost a faction
		}
		add_to_variable = { CHI_rca_civ_war_var = CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var }
		set_variable = { CHI_gov_civ_war_var = 0 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_push_along_yangtze_beijing_wins_tt
	}
	option = {
		name = CHI.lategame.386.b #Nanjing Forces Hold the River

		set_temp_variable = { CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var = CHI_gov_civ_war_var }
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var
			min = 1 #It will always boost a faction
		}
		add_to_variable = { CHI_crs_civ_war_var = CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var }
		set_variable = { CHI_gov_civ_war_var = 0 }

		text = CHI.lategame.390.d.GOV

	}
	desc = {
		text = CHI.lategame.390.d.CRS
		trigger = { CHI_crs_won_civil_war_trigger = yes }
	}
	desc = {
		text = CHI.lategame.390.d.RCA
		trigger = { CHI_rca_won_civil_war_trigger = yes }
	}
	desc = {
		text = CHI.lategame.390.d.PAC #Default Winner
		trigger = { CHI_pac_won_civil_war_trigger = yes }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_intelligence
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	timeout_days = 7

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = CHI_civil_war_over_flag } }

	option = {
		name = CHI.lategame.390.a #Song Qingling's government prevails
		trigger = { CHI_gov_won_civil_war_trigger = yes }

		#Set Up Politics
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Song Qingling"
			desc = "POLITICS_CHI_SONG_QINGLING_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_CHI_Song_Qingling.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = radsoc_tridemism_subtype
		}
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = CHI_Sun_Fo_hog_sli
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var = party_popularity@radical_socialist }
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_neg_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var = CHI_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_neg_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var = -0.75 } #We're gonna subtract about 75% of soc dem popularity
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_add_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var = CHI_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_add_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var = 0.50 } #About 50% of Soc Dem Popularity will turn into Rad Soc
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_add_soc_lib_popularity_temp_var = CHI_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_add_soc_lib_popularity_temp_var = 0.25 } #About 25% of Soc Dem Popularity will turn into Soc Lib
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = CHI_neg_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var }
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = CHI_add_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = CHI_add_soc_lib_popularity_temp_var }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = CHI_revolutionary_committee_party_long
				name = CHI_revolutionary_committee_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = CHI_rca_moderate_party_long
				name = CHI_rca_moderate_party
			}
		}

		#Fallback to ensure characters work okay
		CHI_recruit_PAC_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_recruit_RF_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_recruit_PAC_endgame_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_RCA_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_RCA_generals_effect = yes
		#CRS, RF, and LCS Generals/Advisors Purged later in content

		#Setup Focus Tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_war = no }
			complete_national_focus = CHI_action_now
		}

	}
	option = {
		name = CHI.lategame.390.b #Deng Yanda wipes out the traitors!
		trigger = { CHI_pac_won_civil_war_trigger = yes }

		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}

			name = "Song Qingling"
			desc = "POLITICS_CHI_SONG_QINGLING_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_CHI_Song_Qingling.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"

		}

		set_temp_variable = { CHI_neg_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var = CHI_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_neg_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var = -0.60 } #We're gonna subtract about 75% of soc dem popularity
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_add_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var = CHI_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_add_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var = 0.60 } #About 50% of Soc Dem Popularity will turn into Rad Soc
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = CHI_neg_rad_soc_popularity_temp_var }

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_war_with = CHI }
	}

		name = CHI.lategame.901.a #For our nation and its republic, we reluctantly accept.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 2

					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.75
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 3
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If CHI dwarfs Federalist industry
				factor = 3
				ic_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If FNG/MAN has turtled up by joining Co-Pro - Patriotic Fevor. Only applies if CHI can actually beat them though
				factor = 5
				var:716.owner = {
					is_ally_with = JAP
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = FROM
						ratio < 1
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				CHI = { CHI_Gu_Mengyu_hog = yes }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_will_be_subjugated_tt
		effect_tooltip = { FROM = { china_puppet_ROOT_effect = yes } }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = FROM decision = CHI_betrayal_decision }
		set_country_flag = { flag = CHI_compromise_subjugation_timer_flag days = 180 value = 1 } # Value needs to be there or the effect won't work
		if = {
			limit = { CHI = { CHI_Gu_Mengyu_hog = yes } }
			add_political_power = 25
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -75
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.902 days = 3 } } #A Renewed Republican Alliance
			every_subject_country = {
				country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.904 days = 7 random_days = 7 } #Chen Submits to Nanjing
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = CHI.lategame.901.b #For the good of freedom and democracy, we must decline!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1.3
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 3
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 2
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Measure # of Fed Puppets
				factor = 3
				num_subjects > 2
			}
			modifier = { #Measure # of Fed Puppets
				factor = 5
				num_subjects > 4
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = CHI_ally_betrayal option = CHI_ALLY_BETRAYAL_NEVER }
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_outraged
		}
		add_war_support = -0.10
		FROM = { hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.903 days = 3 } } } #Federalist Talks Reach an Impasse!
	}

				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Assorted Leaders"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = national_populist_subtype
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.asian_tags_array
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_tag_in_china_area = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								tag = UPC
								tag = CHI
							}
						}
						event_target:CHI_UPC_compromise_Fed_leader = {
							CHI_recruit_general_effect = yes
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = { ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								exists = no
								tag = CHI
							}
						}
						CHI = { set_country_flag = GXC_zhang_junmai_joined_CHI }
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Zhang Junmai"
							picture = "gfx/leaders/GXC/Portrait_GXC_Zhang_Junmai.png"
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = market_liberal_subtype
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								exists = no
								tag = CHI
							}
						}
						GXC = { CHI_recruit_li_zongren_effect = yes }
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Li Zongren"
							desc = "POLITICS_GXC_LI_ZONGREN_DESC"
							picture = "gfx/leaders/YUN/Portrait_GXC_Li_Zongren_LKMT.png"
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = pataut_warlordism_subtype
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								exists = no
								tag = CHI
								NOT = { has_unit_leader = 1147 } #Check to see if he's been retired
							}
						}
						SHX = { 
							random_unit_leader = { 
								limit = { has_id = 1147 }
								CHI_recruit_general_effect = yes
							}
						}
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Feng Yuxiang"
							picture = "gfx/leaders/SHX/Portrait_Shanxi_Feng_Yuxiang.png"
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = national_populist_subtype
						}
					}
				}
			}

			set_party_name = { ideology = market_liberal name = CHI_PIP_party long_name = CHI_PIP_party_long }
			set_party_name = { ideology = social_conservative name = CHI_CDL_party long_name = CHI_CDL_party_long }
			set_party_name = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat name = CHI_market_liberal_party long_name = CHI_market_liberal_party_long }
			set_party_name = { ideology = paternal_autocrat name = CHI_rkmt_party long_name = CHI_rkmt_party_long }
			set_party_name = { ideology = national_populist name = CHI_gmj_party long_name = CHI_gmj_party_long }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI.endgame.261.a

		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.04 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.04 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.03 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.02 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = 0.02 }
	}
}

unit_leader_event = {
	id = CHI.endgame.634 #Eagle of the Red Army
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event CHI.endgame.634" }
	title = CHI.endgame.634.t
	desc = CHI.endgame.634.d
	is_triggered_only = yes #fired by on_event related to general promotions.
	trigger = {
		THIS = {
			has_id = 2289
		}
		has_government = totalist
		OR = {
			any_unit_leader = {
				has_id = 2289
				is_unit_leader = yes
				skill > 4
			}
			has_idea = CHI_Lin_Biao_carm
			has_idea = CHI_Lin_Biao_sec_tot
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = CHI.endgame.634.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0.05 }
		set_country_flag = CHI_Lin_Biao_2_carm
		custom_effect_tooltip = unlock_special_carm_minister
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CHI_Lin_Biao_carm }
			hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = CHI_Lin_Biao_carm }
			add_ideas = CHI_Lin_Biao_2_carm
		}
		else = {
			show_ideas_tooltip = CHI_Lin_Biao_2_carm
		}		
	}
	option = {
		name = CHI.endgame.634.b
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.025 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = 0.025 }
	}
}

				}
				country_event = {

					days = 1
				}
				set_country_flag = CHI_Dai_victory_hidden_flag
			}

				limit = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = CHI_Chiang_vs_Dai_Kai_shek_yay
						value > 2
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = chi_tot.13
					days = 1
				}
				set_country_flag = CHI_Chiang_victory_hidden_flag
			}
		}
	}

### Chiang or Dai Victorious ###
country_event = {

	title = {
		text = chi_tot.13.t.kai_shek
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CHI_Chiang_victory_hidden_flag }
	}
	desc = {
		text = chi_tot.13.d.dai
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CHI_Dai_victory_hidden_flag }
	}
	desc = {
		text = chi_tot.13.d.kai_shek
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CHI_Chiang_victory_hidden_flag }
	}
	#picture = GFX_CHI_Chiang_vs_Dai
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Dai Victory
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CHI_Dai_victory_hidden_flag }
		name = chi_tot.13.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_unit_leader = 2000 }
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 2000 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			}
		}
		add_ideas = KR_CHI_Unrest_1
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = KMT_Dai_Rules
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Dai Chunfeng"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHI_DAI_CHUNFENG_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_CHI_Dai_Chunfeng.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = autocratic_socialist_subtype
				traits = { CHI_hooded_chairman_dai }
			}
			complete_national_focus = CHI_lijianzhiye
		}
	}
	option = { # Chiang Victory
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CHI_Chiang_victory_hidden_flag }
		name = chi_tot.13.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		hidden_effect = { retire_country_leader = yes }
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
			desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI_SHEK_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_KMT_Chiang_Kai_shek.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = tot_tridemism_subtype
			traits = { CHI_generalissimo_chiang }
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = KR_focus_dais_rule2
			add_idea = KR_focus_chiangs_rule1
		}
		add_ideas = KR_CHI_Unrest_1
		custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_Chiang_Politics
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = KMT_Chiang_Rules
			set_global_flag = KMT_Chiang_Rules
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_CHIANG
			complete_national_focus = CHI_lijianzhiye
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI_SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_KMT_Chiang_Kai_shek.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = radsoc_tridemism_subtype
				traits = { CHI_generalissimo_chiang }
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI_SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_KMT_Chiang_Kai_shek.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = socdem_tridemism_subtype
				traits = { CHI_generalissimo_chiang }
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Chiang Kai-shek"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHIANG_KAI_SHEK_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_KMT_Chiang_Kai_shek.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = soclib_tridemism_subtype
				traits = { CHI_generalissimo_chiang }
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				long_name = CHI_chiang_nra_long
				name = CHI_chiang_nra
			}
			clr_country_flag = Chiang_Kai_Shek_dead
			clr_country_flag = Chiang_Ching_Kuo_dead
			clr_country_flag = Chiang_Wei_Kuo_dead
			clr_country_flag = Chen_Guofu_dead
			clr_country_flag = Chen_Lifu_dead
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
			add_ideas =  CHI_Chiang_Kai_Shek_hog_tot
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = totalist
				popularity = 0.10
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.10
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = -0.05
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = -0.05
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = chi_tot.14.a
		add_political_power = 100
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_war_support = 0.10
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = KR_focus_dais_rule2
			add_idea = KR_focus_dais_rule3
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_unit_leader = 3000 }
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 3000 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_Dai_Dairect_Marshal
		hidden_effect = {
			create_field_marshal = {
				name = "Dai Chunfeng"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHI_DAI_CHUNFENG_ARMY_DESC"
				portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/CHI/Portrait_CHI_Dai_Chunfeng.png"
				traits = {
					old_guard
					politically_connected
					harsh_leader
					trait_reckless
				}
				skill=1
				attack_skill = 2
				defense_skill = 1
				planning_skill = 2
				logistics_skill = 2
				id = 3001
			}
		}
	}
}

				limit = { has_id = 3001 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_unit_leader = 2201 }
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 2201 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_Chiangs_Subordinates
		hidden_effect = {
			XXA = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_id = 3002
							has_id = 3003
						}
					}
					set_nationality = ROOT
				}
			}			
		}
	}
